<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">позабо́тить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pozabótitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>
<ol><li>to care, to take care, to look after

<li>to worry, to be anxious, to trouble</li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позванивать.html>позва́нивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pozvánivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also  impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ring periodically, to tinkle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:позванивать.html>позва́нивает</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>уша́х</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pozvánivajet</b> v ušáx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">my ears <b>are ringing</b></span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>there is ringing</b> in the ears</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to call (on the phone) periodically</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позволение.html>позволе́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pozvolénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позволение.html>позволе́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позволение.html>позволе́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позволение.html>позволе́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>permission, leave
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:просить.html>проси́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:позволение.html>позволе́ния</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prosítʹ <b>pozvolénija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ask permission</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ваш.html>ва́шего</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:позволение.html>позволе́ния</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s váševo <b>pozvolénija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">with your permission; by your leave</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́тот</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:позволение.html>позволе́ния</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">étot, s <b>pozvolénija</b> skazátʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">this apology for; if one may call him so</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***позвоночник.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:позвоночник.html>позвоно́чник</a> (9384)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позвонок.html>позвоно́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pozvonók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позвоночник.html>позвоно́чник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pozvonóčnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позвоночник.html>позвоно́чника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позвоночник.html>позвоно́чники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позвоночник.html>позвоно́чников</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> backbone, spinal column, vertebral column, spine (set of bones which connected make up the spine and spinal column)</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>зво<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>но́ч<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:относительный.html>относи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a.

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>по́зд<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ний</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 2*a-.
<a href = vnd.unilang:краткий.html>Кра́ткая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a> муж. р. предположительна.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-поздн-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ий</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<ol><li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="разговорное">разг.</span> <i>нареч.</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> поздноватый; <a href = vnd.unilang:довольно.html>дово́льно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поздно.html>по́здно</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:поздний.html>по́зднее</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чем.html>чем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:следовать.html>сле́дует</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чем.html>чем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ожидаться.html>ожида́лось</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><br><span class="example-block" style="color:darkgreen"><a href = vnd.unilang:пожилой.html>Пожило́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дядечка.html>дя́дечка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:недоумение.html>недоуме́нием</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:посмотреть.html>посмотре́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поверх.html>пове́рх</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очко́в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хмыкнуть.html>хмы́кнул</a>: – <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>Да</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:поздновато.html>позднова́то</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:ваш.html>ва́шей</a> Хомке <a href = vnd.unilang:пара.html>пару</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:заводить.html>заводи́ть</a>, отрожала <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свое</a> давным-давно. <span class="example-details" style="font-size:smaller;"> <i>Фаина Раневская, «<a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>Мой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кот.html>кот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пес.html>пес</a>», <span class="example-date">2017</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>г</a>.<span class="citation-source"> </span></i></span></span></span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здороваться.html>здоро́ваться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zdoróvatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поздороваться.html>поздоро́ваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pozdoróvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здороваться.html>здоро́ваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to greet, to salute, to say hello/hi
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Ты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поздороваться.html>поздоро́вался</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:учительница.html>учи́тельницей</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ty <b>pozdoróvalsja</b> s učítelʹnicej?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Did you greet your (female) teacher?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>здо<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ро́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поздравление.html>поздравле́ние</a> (11625)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поздравлять.html>поздравля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pozdravljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поздравление.html>поздравле́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pozdravlénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поздравление.html>поздравле́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поздравление.html>поздравле́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поздравление.html>поздравле́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>congratulation</li></ol>
